Title: Bridging Intermediate- and High-Mass Star Formation with the MIRION Catalog of Yellowballs

Table: Mirion Catalog - Velocities
================================================================================
Byte-by-byte Description of file: tab2.txt
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Bytes  Format Units Label  Explanation
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1-  4  I4     ---     ID        Source identification number
   6- 12  F7.2   km/s    VLSR      Adopted velocity (1)
  14- 17  F4.2   km/s  e_VLSR      Uncertainty in VLSR
  19- 22  A4     ---     SType	   Type of spectrum (2)
  24- 29  F6.2   km/s    VLSR_G    Velocity from GRS (3)
  31- 37  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_S    Velocity from SEDIGISM (3)
  39- 45  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_F    Velocity from FCRAO OGS (3)
  47- 53  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_T    Velocity from ThrUMMS (3)
  55- 61  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_DHT  Velocity from DHT survey (3)
  63- 69  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_DGT  Velocity from dense gas tracer (DGT) survey (3)
  71- 81  A11    ---     DGT       DGT survey (3)
  83- 89  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_C    Velocity reported in Elia et al. (2021)
  91- 97  F7.2   km/s    VLSR_M    Velocity reported in Mege et al. (2021)
  99- 103 F5.2   km/s  e_VLSR_M    Uncertainty in VLSR_M
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Note (1): All velocities are relative to the local standard of rest (LSR)
Note (2): SP = single peak, MP:n = multiple (n) peaks, LSNR = low SNR, and
          OUT = no molecular line survey coverage.
Note (3): See paper for references to all surveys.
